<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:применимый.html>примени́мый</a> (21679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:применить.html>примени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">primenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́мый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:применять.html>применя́ть</a> (2580)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:применить.html>примени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">primenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:применять.html>применя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">primenjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:применить.html>примени́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:примерить.html>приме́ренный</a> (16218)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примерить.html>приме́ренный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">primérennyj</span>)

***примерить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:примерить.html>приме́рить</a> (16218)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерить.html>ме́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">méritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примерить.html>приме́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priméritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примерять.html>примеря́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">приме́ривать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to try on (clothes)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:малыш.html>малы́ш</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:примерить.html>приме́рь</a></b>-ка <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брюки.html>брю́ки</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Malýš, <b>primérʹ</b>-ka éti brjúki.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Kid, try these pants on, will you.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примерять.html>примеря́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">primerjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примерить.html>приме́рить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:примерять.html>приме́рять</a></strong></b>)

<ol><li>to try on (clothes)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красавица.html>краса́вицы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смотреться.html>смотре́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зеркало.html>зе́ркало</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:примерять.html>примеря́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:украшение.html>украше́ния</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Krasávicy smotrélisʹ v zérkalo i <b>primerjáli</b> ukrašénija.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The beauties looked in the mirror and tried on the jewelry.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:примесь.html>при́месь</a> (10899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примесь.html>при́месь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prímesʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примесь.html>при́меси</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примесь.html>при́меси</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примесь.html>при́месей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>admixture, tinge, dash</li>
<li>touch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:примесь.html>при́месью</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>prímesʹju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">with a touch</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">приме́т-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">primét-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примета.html>приме́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priméta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
